 The Reserve Bank on Tuesday asked banks to immediately stop imposing penalty on premature withdrawal of housing loan taken at floating interest rate
 samay se pehle awaas rin lautaane waalon ko isse kaaphi raahat pahonchegi
 The Reserve Bank said in the form sent to the banks, 'it has been decided that the bank will not be allowed to recover penalty on premature withdrawal of housing loan taken at floating interest rates
 ise tatkaal prabhaav se lagu kiya jaataa he
 Referring to the report of the Damodaran Committee, the Reserve Bank said that the loans taken by the banks on the repayment of housing loan before time are not considered as indebted by the banks and there is anger among them
 kendriya bank ke anusaar aisa paaya gaya he ki bank ghatati byaaj dar kii sthiti main kam byaaj dar kaa laabh maujuuda karjadaaron ko nahin dete
 In such a situation, the penalty on repayment of premature housing loan prevents the borrowers from going towards cheap available instruments
 rigerv bank ne kaha ki jurmaana hathaaye jane se maujuuda tathaa naye karjadaaron ke bich bhedbhaav samaapt hoga
 Also, competition among banks will benefit borrowers at floating rates
 kendriya bank ke mutabik, ‘haalanki kai bainkon ne svaichhik rup se samay se purv karj kii vaapasi par jurmaana samaapt kar diya he lekin kuch bainkon ne aisa nahin kiya he
 Therefore, there is a need to bring uniformity in the banking system
 ullekhneey he ki kuch bank philhal bakaaye karj kii samay purv vaapasi par ek se 2 pratishat jurmaana vasuulate hai

 Indira Goswami (1942-2011) Indira Goswami, a well-known storyteller of Assamese, was also known as Mamoni Raisam Goswami in the Northeast
 unhone asamiya logon ke ankahe kashton or dukhon ko apane sahitya ke jariye vaani di
 His creations are known for their variety of plot and distinctive expression skills
 unhone schuli jivan se hi kahani lekhan shuru kar diya tha
 His early story collections are Chinaki Maram and Kaina
 baad main hriday ek nadeer naam, nirvaachit galp or priy galp sheershakon se unke kahani sangrah bhi prakashit-prashansit hue
 Goswami binds readers sensitively rather than emotionally in her stories
 unki kritiyon ke vistrut falak main manushya jivan apane vaividhya or vilakshantaa ke saath maujuud he
 His stories have a confluence of real, subtle insight and deep poetic senses
 yahi tathy goswami ke upanyaason ke liye bhi sahi he
 His first novel was the Chenabar source
 parvarti kaal main unke jo upanyaas apane utkrisht str or marmasparshi style ke kaaran bahucharchit hue ve hai nilkanth braj, ahiran, maamare dhara tarowal, sanskaar, ishwar jakhmi jatri, jej aaru dhuli dhoosarit prishth, dasarthir khoj or chinmasta
 His novel Datal Hathir Une Khova Howda attained the status of a classic
 goswami ne mahaj 27 saal kii umr main aatmakatha aadha lekha dastavej likhi
 This brought him to the top of fame
 iskaa desh-videsh kii kai bhashaaon main anuwaad hua
 Her autobiography came at a time when she was feeling completely alone
 aktubar 1965 main unki shaadi hui thi or 1967 main unke pati madhavan raisam ayyangar kii jeep durghatana main maut ho gai
 The happiness of married life was found only for one and a half years
 pati kii maut ne unhen gahare avsaad main daal diya
 He also attempted suicide but failed
 avsaad kaa saamana karne ke liye unhone swayan ko lekhan main vyast kar diya or usee se ghaatak avsaad par kaabo paa sakin
 He received several accolades, including the Sahitya Akademi and the Jnanpith Award for his outstanding contribution to literature
 peshey se ve shikshak thim
 She was an Assamese professor in the Indian Language Department of the University of Delhi
 goswami ne assam ke ugravadiyon ke antarman ko samajha or centre sarkaar or ugravadiyon ke bich shantivaarta kii madhyasthata bhi kii

 odisha ke malkangiri jile main shuukravaar ko naksaliyon ne seemaa suraksha bal (biguef) ke ek vaahan ko visphot se uda diya
 Four officers of the force were killed in this attack and two others were seriously injured
 police mahanireekshak (oparations) wibi khurania ne bataaya ki naksaliyon ne desi bam (iidi) kaa istemaal karte hue balimela ke sameep visphot ko anjaam diya
 He told, "four security officers were martyred in this attack
 " unhone bataaya ki shahid suraksha adhikariyon main biguef 107 batalian ke ek commandent, ek dipti commandent, ek inspector or ek sahaayak upanireekshak shaamil hai
 The attack took place while security officers were traveling to their base in a private multi-utility vehicle
 tippaniyan One soldier and the driver of the vehicle survived, but his condition remains critical
 ullekhneey he ki bhubaneshwar se kareeb 600 kilometre kii duuri par sthit malkangiri jila naksaliyon kaa garh mana jaataa he
 Inspector General of Police (operations) YB Khurania said that the Naxals carried out the blast near Balimela using indigenous bombs (ieds)
 unhone bataaya, "is hamale main chaar suraksha adhikari shahid hue
 "he said the martyred security officers included a commandant of BSF 107 battalion, a deputy commandant, an inspector and an assistant sub-inspector
 hamalaa us samay kiya gaya jab suraksha adhikari ek nijee bahuupayogi vaahan se apane adde par ja rahe the
 The comments ek sipaahi or vaahan kaa chaalak kii jaan batch gai lekin unki haalat naajak bani hui he
 It is noteworthy that Malkangiri district, located about 600 km from Bhubaneswar, is considered a stronghold of Naxalites

 haal hi main shahid ne neha dhoopiya ke chat sho Vogue bffs main ranvir ke ek behad charchit gane kaa hissaa hone kii manshaa jataai

 Sahara has received a major setback from the Supreme Court
 supreme court ne sahaara ko niveshkon kii sahi suchi saunpane ke nirdesh die hai or ek hafte ke bheetar suchi maangi he
 The next hearing of the case will be on 2 May
 supreme court ne sebi dwaara daayar avmaananaa maamle main jawaab nahin dene ke kaaran sahaara samooh or uske mukhiya subrat roy ko aade haath liya
 Significantly, SEBI had registered a case against two companies of Sahara and instructed to hand over the list of investors
 sahaara samooh ne sebi kii apil par 22 april ko hone vaali sunwaayee ko taalane ke liye supreme court kaa darwaja khatkhataya
 SEBI had filed an application from the court to detain Sahara Group President Subrata Roy Sahara and initiate contempt proceedings against him
 nyaayamurti ke es radhakrishnan ke netritv main khandpeeth ne kaha tha ki vah 22 april ko yah faisla legi ki sahaara kii yachika par vichaar kiya jaye yaa nahin
 On March 15, SEBI moved the Supreme Court seeking a stay on the arrest of Sahara Group chief Subrata Roy Sahara and his leaving the country
 sahaara samooh kii do companiyon ne apane niveshkon ko 24 hajaar karod rupee waapas karne ke aadesh kaa paalan nahin kiya tha
 SEBI had sought permission from the court to arrest and detain Sahara owner Subrata Sahara
 chah farvari ko court ne sahaara samooh ko notice jari kiya tha or yah kehete huye chaar saptaah main jawaab maanga tha ki unke khilaaf avmaananaa kii kaarywahi kyon na shuru kii jaye
 The court also said that SEBI is free to seize the accounts and assets of two Sahara Group companies
 yah do companiyaan hai- sahaara india real estate kaperereshan or sahaara houseing investment coperereshan

 harshavardhan ne 27 june ko ye kahkar ek vivadako janm de diya tha ki skulon main sex ajukeshan par bain lagava diya jaae

 is video ko 14 july ko post kiya gaya or abhi tak ise 2

 soshal media par ise jamkar share kiya ja rahaa he

 lekin saath hi ye bhi kehete hai ki agar ladki paidaa ho jaae to khap panchayat ke paas ritern policy bhi hoti he

 iske liye dekhen puraa videoh Expressing concern over the slow pace of the trial against the perpetrators of the Mumbai attacks, India said on Thursday that many "real accused" individuals had not been brought before Pakistani courts
 grih sachiv aarake singh ne apane pakistani samakaksh ke saath vaarta ke liye jane se pehle media se sankshipt vaartalap main kaha, ‘‘aisa lagata he ki unke :mumbai hamalon ke aropiyon: khilaaf nyaayik kaarywahi kii gati kaaphi dhimi he
 Many people, who are the real accused, have not been brought before the courts
 ’’ bharat or pakistan ke grih sachivon ke bich do din tak chalane vaali vaarta main vija niyamon ko saral banane or lashkar-e-taiyaba dwaara kiye gaye mumbai hamalon ke aropiyon ke mukademe par dhyaan kendrit kiye jane kii ummid he
 Indian officials linked several serving and retired officers of the Pakistani Army to the Mumbai attacks on the basis of evidence provided by lashkar-e-taiba pakistani-american activist David Coleman Headley
 haalanki, pakistan in aaropon ko khaarij kar chukaa he
 Pakistan has not responded positively to India's request to provide voice samples of suspects already in their custody
 grih sachiv aarake singh ke netritv main bhartiya dal or pakistan ke grih sachiv khwaja siddiq akbar ke netritv main pakistani dal ke adhikari islamabad ke ek hotel main ekatrit hue
 The last round of talks between the Home Secretaries of the two countries was held in New Delhi in March last year
 bhartiya pratinidhimandal main rashtriya jaanch agency (enie) ke pramukh es si sinha or 2008 ke mumbai hamale kii jaanch kar rahe anya mahatvapurn adhikariyon ko shaamil kiya janaa bharat ke iraadon kaa spasht sanket he ki mumbai kii vyavsaayik rajdhani par hamale ke shadyantrkariyon par mukademe ko aage le jaaya jaae
 In the Mumbai attacks, seven Pakistani nationals, including lashkar-e-taiba commander Zakiur Rehman Lakhvi, have been charged with planning, financing and executing the attacks
 haalanki, rawalpindi kii aatankwaad nirodhi adaalat main vibhinn takneekee kaarnon se un par chal rahaa mukadmaa ek saal se adhik samay se sthagit padaa he
 Despite the visit of the Pakistani judicial team to India in March for the purpose of gathering evidence and recording the statements of Indian officials, there has been no progress in the trial in recent weeks
 bharat dwaara lashkar e taiyaba ke sansthaapak hafiz mohammad said ke khilaaf karrwai kii maang nae sire se kiye jane kii ummid he jiske khilaaf america ne ek karod america dollar ke inaam kii ghoshnaa kii he
 Pakistan has claimed that the evidence provided by India is not sufficient for legal action against Saeed, who has held several big rallies against the US and India in recent months
 vaarta se pehle bhartiya adhikariyon ne kaha ki donon pakshon ne nae aasaan vija niyamon ko antim rup de diya he jinamein pehali baar paryatak vija, varisht nagarikon or bacchon ko aagaman par vija tathaa vyavsaayiyon ke liye ek saal tak kaa bahu pravesh vija shaamil hai
 The two home secretaries are expected to sign an mou at the conclusion of the talks tomorrow
 haalanki, pakistani media main ai kuch khabaron main daawa kiya gaya he ki vija samjhaute par dastakhat hone kii sambhaavna nahin he kyonki pakistani mantrimandal ne kal apni baithak main ise manjuuri nahin di
 Reports said that Home Minister Rehman Malik did not put the agreement before the cabinet for approval
 grih mantralay ke ek agyaat adhikari ke hawaale se nesan akhbaar ne kaha ki adhikariyon ne grih sachivon kii agali baithak tak nae vija samjhaute par hastakshar main vilamb karne kaa faisla kiya he
 The two countries have been working on a draft new visa agreement for over a year
 bharat aatankwaad, maadak padaatharen kii taskari, bharat se bhagkar pakistan main chhipe daud ibrahim or indian mujahidin aatankiyon jaise bhagodon, bharat main nakli mudra chalaane vaale network or donon deshon kii jelon main band kaidiyon kii rihaai jaise anya mahatvapurn muddon par bhi charchaa karegaa
 The comments aath april ko pakistani raashtrapati asif ali jaradaari kii bharat yatra ke dauraan pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne pakistan se aatankwaad par lagaam lagane ke liye thos karrwai karne ko kaha tha, taaki bharat dwipaksheeya sambandhon kii disha main aage bad sake
 Manmohan also asked the conspirators of the Mumbai attacks to be brought to justice
 pakistan kii ore se samjhauta express train visphot ke jimmedaar logon ke khilaaf karrwai karne kii baat kahe jane kii ummid he jisamen 42 pakistaniyon sahit kareeb 70 log maare gaye the
 "it seems that the pace of judicial proceedings against him (accused of Mumbai attacks) is slowing down," Home Secretary RK Singh said in a brief conversation with the media before going for talks with his Pakistani counterpart
 bahut se log, jo asal aaropee hai, adaalaton ke samaksh tak nahin laae ja sake hai
 The two-day-long talks between the home secretaries of India and Pakistan are expected to simplify visa rules and focus on the trial of accused in the Mumbai attacks carried out by lashkar-e-taiba
 bhartiya adhikariyon ne lashkar-e-taiyaba ke pakistani america kaaryakarta david colman hedli dwaara uplabdh karaae gaye saakshyon ke aadhaar par pakistani sena ke kai sevarat or sevanivrutt adhikariyon kaa sambandh mumbai hamalon se joda tha
 However, Pakistan has denied these allegations
 pakistan ne pehle se hi apni hiraasat main band sandigdhon kii aawaaj ke namoonay dene ke bharat ke aagrah kaa sakaaratmak jawaab nahin diya he
 Indian contingent led by Home Secretary RK Singh and Pakistani contingent led by Pakistan Home Secretary Khwaja Siddique Akbar gathered at a hotel in Islamabad
 donon deshon ke grih sachivon ke bich pichley daur kii vaarta gat varsh march main nayi dilli main hui thi
 The Indian delegation's inclusion of National Investigation Agency (NIA) chief SC Sinha and other key officials probing the 2008 Mumbai attack is a clear indication of India's intentions to pursue the case against the conspirators of the attack on the commercial capital of Mumbai
 Be taken mumbai hamalon main lashkar e taiyaba ke commander jackieur rahamaan lakhvi sahit saat pakistani nagarikon par hamalon kii yojana banane, vittiya madad karne or anjaam dene kaa aarope lagaaya gaya he
 However, his trial in the anti-terrorism court in Rawalpindi has been adjourned for more than a year due to various technical reasons
 sakshya jutaney or bhartiya adhikariyon ke bayaan darj karne ke uddeshy se march main pakistani nyaayik dal ke bharat daure ke baavjood haal ke hafton main mukademe main koi pragati nahin hui he
 India is expected to demand fresh action against lashkar-e-taiba founder Hafiz Mohammed Saeed, against which the US has announced a reward of ten million US dollars
 pakistan ne daawa kiya he ki bharat dwaara uplabdh karaae gaye sakshya said ke khilaaf kanoonee karrwai ke liye paryaapt nahin hai jisane haal ke maheenon main america or bharat ke khilaaf kai badi reliyaan kii hai
 Prior to the talks, Indian officials said the two sides have finalized new easy visa rules, including tourist visas for the first time, visas for senior citizens and children on arrival and multi-year visas for businessmen up to one year
 donon grih sachivon ke kal vaarta ke samaapan par ek sahmati patr par hastakshar karne kii ummid he
 However, some reports in Pakistani media claimed that the visa agreement is unlikely to be signed as the Pakistani cabinet did not approve it in its meeting yesterday
 khabaron main kaha gaya ki grahamantri rahamaan malik ne samjhaute ko manjuuri ke liye mantrimandal ke samaksh nahin rakhaa
 Quoting an undisclosed Home Ministry official, the Nation newspaper said that the authorities have decided to delay the signing of the new visa agreement till the next meeting of Home Secretaries
 donon desh ek saal se adhik samay se nae vija samjhaute ke masaude par kaam kar rahe hai
 India will also discuss other important issues such as terrorism, drug trafficking, fugitives such as Dawood Ibrahim and Indian Mujahideen terrorists fleeing from India, fake currency-running networks in India and the release of prisoners held in jails of both countries
 tippaniyan During the visit of Pakistani President Asif Ali Zardari to India on April 8, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh asked Pakistan to take concrete action to curb terrorism so that India can move forward in bilateral relations
 manmohan ne mumbai hamalon ke sajeeshkartaaon ko nyaay ke kathghare main bhi laane ko kaha tha
 Pakistan is expected to act against those responsible for the Samjhauta Express train blast in which around 70 people, including 42 Pakistanis, were killed
